moment at point C in the simply supported beam. Point C is
located just to the right of the 2.5-kN # m couple moment.
B
A 30
C

2 m 2 m

+↑ΣF = 0;

(cid:2)+ ΣM

Determine the distance abetween the bearings in terms of w
the shaft’s length L so that the moment in the symmetric
shaft is zero at its center.
a
L
SOLUTION
Due to symmetry,A y = B y
w(L - a) w(L - a)
+c©F y = 0; A y + B y - 4 - wa - 4 = 0
w
A y = B y = 4 (L + a)
wa a w(La) a L a w a
a+©M = 0; -M - - + - + (L + a) = 0
2 a4b 4 a2 6 6b 4 a2b
Since M = 0;
3a2 + (L - a)(L + 2a) - 3a(L + a) = 0
2a2 + 2aL - L2 = 0
a = 0.366L Ans.
Ans:
a = 0.366L

7–51.  Continued
The support reactions are indicated on the FBD of the beam, Fig. a. Since the
loading discontinues, the shear and moment functions must be written for regions
| 0 … x 6 2 m and 2 m | 6 x … 6 m of the beam. The FBD of the beam’s segment  |     |     |     |
| ------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------- | --- | --- | --- |
sectioned through an arbitrary point in these two regions are shown in Fig. b and c.
| For region 0 …  | x 6 2 m, Fig. b, |            |     |     |
| --------------- | ---------------- | ---------- | --- | --- |
| +cΣF = 0;  20.0 | - V = 0  V       | = 20.0 kN  |     | (1) |
y
| a+ΣM 0;  M     | 20.0x 0  M     | {20.0x} kN | # m  | (2) |
| -------------- | -------------- | ---------- | ---- | --- |
| =              | - =            | =          |      |     |
| For region 2 m | x 6 m, Fig. c, |            |      |     |
6 …
| +cΣF = 0;  V | + 10.0 = 0  V | = -10.0 kN  |     | (3) |
| ------------ | ------------- | ----------- | --- | --- |
y
| a+ΣM         |          |                |             | #      |
| ------------ | -------- | -------------- | ----------- | ------ |
| = 0;  10.0(6 | - x) - M | = 0  M = {60.0 | - 10.0x} kN | m  (4) |
The shear diagram shown in Fig. d is plotted using Eqs. (1) and (3), while the moment
diagram shown in Fig. e is plotted using Eqs. (2) and (4). The value of moment at
x = 2 m can be evaluated using either Eqs. (2) or (4).
